# AAP 2.4 — Rpm Install Playbook Tasks

Task execution order for the AAP install playbook, expanded recursively through included roles and task files. Conditional tasks include a `When` column; tasks inside blocks inherit the block condition. **Progress** runs from 0% (first row) to 100% (last row) based on position in the expanded task list.

| Field | Value |
|-------|-------|
| Playbook command | `./setup.sh -i inventory` |
| Source playbook | `collections/ansible_collections/ansible/automation_platform_installer/playbooks/install.yml` |
| Installer dump | `.installer-dumps/2.4/ansible-automation-platform-setup-2.4-16` |
| Total tasks (expanded) | 2031 |

## Notes

- **Location** shows the play and role/task-file breadcrumb path from `install.yml`.
- The same role or task file may appear multiple times when invoked from different plays or blocks.
- Recursive cycles (A includes B includes A) are detected and marked as skipped.
- Handler tasks (`notify`) are not executed inline; they run when notified and flushed.
- **Progress** runs from 0% (first row) to 100% (last row).
- **Do not Format Document** on this file — Markdown table formatters pad every column to the widest cell (~400+ char lines). Regenerate with `python3 installer/scripts/extract_install_playbook_tasks.py` instead.
- Inventories in this folder are co-located with this reference — `@`-mention `installer/AAP{XY}/{method}/` for both.
- OpenShift operator examples are in the sibling [`openshift/`](../../../openshift/) folder (no install playbook).
